<script type="text/javascript">
    // <![CDATA[
    $('#upload_button').click(function () {
        build_destination_url()
    });

        var base_url = "http://www.imagebam.com/sys/upload/flashsave/0/goc0pioshhiqe58xyqzxx18eemca1t9i/d3c3c8c4c71c78239656f37e8e191412";
    var new_gallery_id = "imi7460moic3ol1mb1k82tnhfzsht1zb";


    var uploader = new plupload.Uploader({
        runtimes: 'flash,html5,html4',
        browse_button: 'pickfiles',
        container: 'container',
        max_file_size: '10mb',
        url: 'upload.php',
        flash_swf_url: '/JS/Moxie.swf',
        filters: [
            {title: "Image files", extensions: "jpg,jpeg,gif,png,JPG,JPEG,GIF,PNG"}
        ]
    });

    uploader.bind('Init', function (up, params) {

    });

    $('#uploadfiles').click(function (e) {

        //uploader.start();
        getURL();
        e.preventDefault();
    });

    uploader.init();

    uploader.bind('FilesAdded', function (up, files) {
        $.each(files, function (i, file) {
            $('#filelist').append(
                '<div id="' + file.id + '" class="filecontainer">' +
                '<div class="filename">' + file.name + '</div>' +
                '<div class="filesize">' + plupload.formatSize(file.size) + '</div>' +
                '<div class="filestatus" id="status_' + file.id + '">0%</div>' +
                '<div class="filedel"><a id="remove_' + file.id + '" href="#"><img src="/img/icons/bin_closed.png" alt=""/></a></div><div></div>' +
                '</div>');

            $('#remove_' + file.id).click(function (e) {
                uploader.removeFile(file)
                $('#' + file.id).remove();
            });
        });


        up.refresh(); // Reposition Flash/Silverlight

        $('#filelist').animate({
                scrollTop: $('#filelist').attr("scrollHeight")
            },
            1500);
    });

    uploader.bind('UploadProgress', function (up, file) {
        $('#status_' + file.id).html(file.percent + "%");

        $('#percent').width(uploader.total.percent + "%");
        $('#percent_text').text(uploader.total.percent + "%");
        $('#upRate').text(Math.ceil(uploader.total.bytesPerSec / 1024) + " kb/sec");

    });

    uploader.bind('Error', function (up, err) {
        if (err.code == '-600') {
            file = err.file;
            $('#' + file.id).remove();

            $('#filelist').append("<div class='fileerror'>The file " + err.file.name + " is too large.</div>");


        } else {
            $('#filelist').append("<div class='fileerror'>Error: " + err.code +
                ", Message: " + err.message +
                (err.file ? ", File: " + err.file.name : "") +
                "</div>"
            );
        }


        up.refresh(); // Reposition Flash/Silverlight
    });

    uploader.bind('FileUploaded', function (up, file) {
        $('#' + file.id + " b").html("100%");

        if (this.total.queued == 0) {
            $('#redirectform').submit();
            $('#upload_info').html("<div style='text-align:center; font-size:14px; font-weight:bold;'>Almost Done! Photos Processing...</div>");
        }

    });


    // ]]>
</script>

  <script>
    var c = 0;

    function rnd(start, end) {
      return Math.floor(Math.random() * (end - start + 1) + start);
    }

    function change() {
      console.log($(".tmpl").length);
      var n = rnd(0, 4);
      while (c == n) {
        n = rnd(0, 4);
      }
      c = n;

      $(".tmpl").each(function (index, el) {
        console.log(n);
        if (index == n) {
          $("div .photo5").html($(this).html());
        }
      });

    }
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
    var intervalId = null;

    function slideAd(id, nStayTime, sState, nMaxHth, nMinHth) {
      this.stayTime = nStayTime * 2000 || 2000;
      this.maxHeigth = nMaxHth || 320;
      this.minHeigth = nMinHth || 2.5;
      this.state = sState || "down";
      var obj = document.getElementById(id);
      if (intervalId != null) window.clearInterval(intervalId);

      function openBox() {
        var h = obj.offsetHeight;
        obj.style.height = ((this.state == "down") ? (h + 4) : (h - 10)) + "px";
        if (obj.offsetHeight > this.maxHeigth) {
          window.clearInterval(intervalId);
          intervalId = window.setInterval(closeBox, this.stayTime);
        }
        if (obj.offsetHeight < this.minHeigth) {
          window.clearInterval(intervalId);
          obj.style.display = "none";
        }
      }

      function closeBox() {
        slideAd(id, this.stayTime, "up", nMaxHth, nMinHth);
      }
      intervalId = window.setInterval(openBox, 10);
    }
  </script>
  <!--手动下拉代码js-->
</head>

    $(function () {
      $('.ms-list-item dd').hover(
        function () {
          $(this).children('ul').css({
            display: 'block'
          });
          $(this).focus().css({
            background: 'url(http://www.sznews.com/resource/templateRes/201909/24/1056/1056/ms-icon-l-minus.png) no-repeat 285px 15px'

  <script type="text/javascript">
    $(function () {

      var stringTime = "2016-12-12 00:00:00";
      var timestamp2 = Date.parse(new Date(stringTime));

      var stringTime = "2016-12-14 00:00:00";
      var timestamp3 = Date.parse(new Date(stringTime));

      var timestamp = Date.parse(new Date());

      if (timestamp > timestamp2 && timestamp < timestamp3) {
        console.log("ds");
        layer.ready(function () {
          layer.open({
            type: 1,
            shade: 0,
            title: false, //不显示标题
            content: $('#advPrev'), //捕获的元素
            time: 15000,
            // anim:1,
            shift: 2,
            closeBtn: 0,
            offset: 'rb',
            btnAlign: 'l',
            cancel: function (index) {
              layer.close(index);
              this.content.show();
              $("#advPrev").hide();
            }
          });
        });

        $("#advPrev").show(function () {
          var advtime = 15;

          var advtimer = setInterval(function () {
            advtime--;
            $(".adv-time").text(advtime);
            if (advtime <= 0) {
              clearInterval(advtimer);
            }

          }, 1000);
        });

        $(".close-adv").click(function () {
          $("#advPrev").hide();
        });
      }
    });
  </script>

<script>
  //处理“天天3.15消费投诉”征集的提交事件
  $(function () {
    var btn = document.getElementById("complain315SubmitBtn");
    var t1 = document.getElementById("TextBox1");
    var t2 = document.getElementById("TextBox2");
    var t3 = document.getElementById("TextBox3");
    var t6 = document.getElementById("TextBox6");
    //添加隐藏域
    $("input#__VIEWSTATE").val(
      "/wEPDwUKMTY5MDk3NDM2NQ9kFgICAw8WAh4HZW5jdHlwZQUTbXVsdGlwYXJ0L2Zvcm0tZGF0YWRk8+PH4SFfr8sC1w3qtVAxsKBYaSg=");
    $("input#__EVENTVALIDATION").val(
      "/wEWCAKowefRDgLs0bLrBgLs0fbZDALs0Yq1BQLs0e58AuzRgtgJAuzRxsYPAoznisYGQGcJ9njOlmW8htwdqVamBGCSpUI=");
    btn.onclick = function (event) {
      if (t1.value == "" || t2.value == "" || t3.value == "" || t6.value == "") {
        alert("请填写完整信息");
        returnFunc();
        return;
      }
      if (!/^1[34578][0-9]{9}$/.test(t6.value)) {
        alert("请填写正确的手机号");
        returnFunc();
        return;
      }

      function returnFunc() {
        event.preventDefault();
      }
    };

    var iframe = document.getElementById("hide_frame");
    if (iframe.attachEvent) {
      iframe.attachEvent("onload", tip); // IE
    } else {
      iframe.onload = tip; // 非IE
    }

    function tip() {
      if (t1.value == "") return;
      t1.value = "";
      t2.value = "";
      t3.value = "";
      t6.value = "";
    };
  });
</script>
